      FROM users AS u
      INNER JOIN roles AS r ON u.role_id = r.id
      LEFT JOIN (
          SELECT u0.id, u0.created_at, u0.location_id, u0.user_id, l.id AS id0, l.address, l.code, l.created_at AS created_at0, l.is_active, l.name, l.updated_at
          FROM user_locations AS u0
          INNER JOIN locations AS l ON u0.location_id = l.id
      ) AS s ON u.id = s.user_id
      ORDER BY u.full_name, u.id, r.id, s.id

      SELECT i.id AS "Id", i.lot_number AS "LotNumber", i0.item_name AS "ItemName", i0.peroxide_class AS "PeroxideClass", l.name AS "LabName", l0.name AS "LocationName", i.open_date AS "OpenDate", i.first_inspect_date AS "FirstInspectDate", i.last_monitor_date AS "LastMonitorDate", i.next_monitor_date AS "NextMonitorDate", i.peroxide_status AS "PeroxideStatus", i.quantity_remaining AS "QuantityRemaining", i.unit AS "Unit", i.status AS "Status", CASE
          WHEN i.next_monitor_date IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(date_part('epoch', date_trunc('day', i.next_monitor_date) - date_trunc('day', now() AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')) / 86400.0 AS integer)
      END AS "DaysUntilDue"
      FROM inventory_lots AS i
      INNER JOIN items AS i0 ON i.item_id = i0.id
      INNER JOIN labs AS l ON i.lab_id = l.id
      INNER JOIN locations AS l0 ON i.location_id = l0.id
      WHERE i0.requires_peroxide_monitoring AND i.status <> 'consumed' AND i.status <> 'disposed' AND i.status <> 'expired'
      ORDER BY CASE
          WHEN CASE
              WHEN i.next_monitor_date IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(date_part('epoch', date_trunc('day', i.next_monitor_date) - date_trunc('day', now() AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')) / 86400.0 AS integer)
          END IS NOT NULL THEN CASE
              WHEN i.next_monitor_date IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(date_part('epoch', date_trunc('day', i.next_monitor_date) - date_trunc('day', now() AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')) / 86400.0 AS integer)
          END
          ELSE 2147483647
      END

      SELECT p3.id, p3.classification, p3.created_at, p3.inventory_lot_id, p3.next_monitor_due, p3.notes, p3.ppm_result, p3.result_text, p3.result_type, p3.test_date, p3.test_method, p3.tested_by_user_id, p3.visual_observations
      FROM (
          SELECT p.inventory_lot_id
          FROM peroxide_tests AS p
          WHERE p.inventory_lot_id = ANY (@__lotIds_0)
          GROUP BY p.inventory_lot_id
      ) AS p1
      LEFT JOIN (
          SELECT p2.id, p2.classification, p2.created_at, p2.inventory_lot_id, p2.next_monitor_due, p2.notes, p2.ppm_result, p2.result_text, p2.result_type, p2.test_date, p2.test_method, p2.tested_by_user_id, p2.visual_observations
          FROM (
              SELECT p0.id, p0.classification, p0.created_at, p0.inventory_lot_id, p0.next_monitor_due, p0.notes, p0.ppm_result, p0.result_text, p0.result_type, p0.test_date, p0.test_method, p0.tested_by_user_id, p0.visual_observations, ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY p0.inventory_lot_id ORDER BY p0.created_at DESC) AS row
              FROM peroxide_tests AS p0
              WHERE p0.inventory_lot_id = ANY (@__lotIds_0)
          ) AS p2

      ) AS p3 ON p1.inventory_lot_id = p3.inventory_lot_id

      SELECT i.id AS "Id", i.lot_number AS "LotNumber", i0.item_name AS "ItemName", i0.peroxide_class AS "PeroxideClass", l.name AS "LabName", l0.name AS "LocationName", i.open_date AS "OpenDate", i.first_inspect_date AS "FirstInspectDate", i.last_monitor_date AS "LastMonitorDate", i.next_monitor_date AS "NextMonitorDate", i.peroxide_status AS "PeroxideStatus", i.quantity_remaining AS "QuantityRemaining", i.unit AS "Unit", i.status AS "Status", CASE
          WHEN i.next_monitor_date IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(date_part('epoch', date_trunc('day', i.next_monitor_date) - date_trunc('day', now() AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')) / 86400.0 AS integer)
      END AS "DaysUntilDue"
      FROM inventory_lots AS i
      INNER JOIN items AS i0 ON i.item_id = i0.id
      INNER JOIN labs AS l ON i.lab_id = l.id
      INNER JOIN locations AS l0 ON i.location_id = l0.id
      WHERE i0.requires_peroxide_monitoring AND i.status <> 'consumed' AND i.status <> 'disposed' AND i.status <> 'expired'
      ORDER BY CASE
          WHEN CASE
              WHEN i.next_monitor_date IS NOT NULL THEN CAST(date_part('epoch', date_trunc('day', i.next_monitor_date) - date_trunc('day', now() AT TIME ZONE 'UTC')) / 86400.0 AS integer)
          END IS NOT NULL THEN CASE

          END

      END
